</tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 7\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 10\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         85\xc2\xa0mph (140\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         981\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Franklin" title="Hurricane Franklin">\n        Hurricane Franklin\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The NHC began tracking a tropical wave in the southeastern Caribbean Sea for possible\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclogenesis" title="Tropical cyclogenesis">\n        development\n       </a>\n       on August 3.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After organizing for a few days, advisories were initiated on Potential Tropical Cyclone Seven at 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August 6.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-d1_79-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-d1-79">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disturbance became Tropical Storm Franklin at 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August 7.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-d2_80-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-d2-80">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After strengthening into a moderate tropical storm, Franklin made its first landfall near Pulticub, Mexico at 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August 8.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1stlandfallfranklin_81-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-1stlandfallfranklin-81">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The cyclone weakened considerably while over the peninsula, however its satellite presentation remained well-defined, with the inner core tightening up considerably.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-d7_82-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-d7-82">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later that day, Franklin emerged into the Bay of Campeche, and immediately began strengthening again, becoming a hurricane late on August\xc2\xa09.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-83">\n        <a href="#cite_note-83">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Five hours after peaking in intensity with winds of 85\xc2\xa0mph (140\xc2\xa0km/h) and a pressure of 981\xc2\xa0mbar (28.97\xc2\xa0inHg),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">\n        <a href="#cite_note-84">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Franklin made landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Vega_de_Alatorre" title="Vega de Alatorre">\n        Lechuguillas, Mexico\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">\n        <a href="#cite_note-85">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and thereafter began to rapidly weaken. By 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa010, Franklin had dissipated as a tropical cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, its mid-level circulation remained intact and later contributed to the formation of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Jova_(2017)" title="Tropical Storm Jova (2017)">\n        Tropical Storm Jova\n       </a>\n       in the Eastern Pacific early on August\xc2\xa012.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Jova_87-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Jova-87">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Immediately upon classification of Franklin as a potential tropical cyclone,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_storm_warning" title="Tropical storm warning">\n        tropical storm warnings\n       </a>\n       were issued for much of the eastern side of the Yucat\xc3\xa1n Peninsula on August 6;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-d1_79-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-d1-79">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       a small portion of the coastline was upgraded to a hurricane watch with the possibility of Franklin nearing hurricane intensity as it approached the coastline the next night. Approximately 330 people were reported as going into storm shelters, and around 2,200 relocated from the islands near the coastline to farther inland in advance of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-impacts1_88-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-impacts1-88">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the Mexican part of the peninsula, damage was reported as having being minimal, mainly in Belize as the storm tracked slightly more northwards then expected, lessening impacts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-impacts1_88-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-impacts1-88">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nonetheless, some areas received up to a foot of rain.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Gert">\n        Hurricane Gert\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Hurricane Gert">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gert_2017-08-16_Suomi_NPP.jpg">\n            <img alt="Gert 2017-08-16 Suomi NPP.jpg" data-file-height="3300" data-file-width="2270" height="218" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Gert_2017-08-16_Suomi_NPP.jpg/150px-Gert_2017-08-16_Suomi_NPP.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Gert_2017-08-16_Suomi_NPP.jpg/225px-Gert_2017-08-16_Suomi_NPP.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/15/Gert_2017-08-16_Suomi_NPP.jpg/300px-Gert_2017-08-16_Suomi_NPP.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Gert_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Gert 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1669" data-file-width="2700" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Gert_2017_track.png/150px-Gert_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Gert_2017_track.png/225px-Gert_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a1/Gert_2017_track.png/300px-Gert_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 13\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 August 17\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         105\xc2\xa0mph (165\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         967\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On August\xc2\xa02, the NHC began monitoring a tropical wave and its associated convection over the western coast of Africa.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the disturbance tracked west-northwest, its structure changed little in organization, but environmental conditions were expected to support the formation of a tropical cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-91">\n        <a href="#cite_note-91">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Instead, the system remained poorly defined and entered a less conducive environment east of the Leeward Islands.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After progressing into the southwestern Atlantic several days later, the wave encountered more favorable upper-level winds and began to show signs of organization.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Following the formation of a well-defined circulation, the disturbance was upgraded to a tropical depression at 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa013;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       by 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC that afternoon, it intensified into Tropical Storm Gert.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa015, Gert intensified to a Category\xc2\xa01 hurricane with maximum sustained winds of 75\xc2\xa0mph (120\xc2\xa0km/h), making it the second hurricane of the season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-96">\n        <a href="#cite_note-96">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Accelerating east-northeastwards, Gert peaked as a Category\xc2\xa02 system early on August\xc2\xa017 at an unusually high latitude of 40\xc2\xb0N.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Thereafter, Gert began to rapidly weaken as it shifted from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Gulf_Stream" title="Gulf Stream">\n        Gulf Stream\n       </a>\n       over cooler waters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-98">\n        <a href="#cite_note-98">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Just 12\xc2\xa0hours after achieving peak intensity, Gert weakened below hurricane status and evolved to an extratropical cyclone well east of\n       <a href="/wiki/Nova_Scotia" title="Nova Scotia">\n        Nova Scotia\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">\n        <a href="#cite_note-99">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Two people drowned due to strong rip currents produced by the hurricane: one in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_Banks" title="Outer Banks">\n        Outer Banks\n       </a>\n       of North Carolina, and the other in\n       <a href="/wiki/Nantucket,_Massachusetts" title="Nantucket, Massachusetts">\n        Nantucket, Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">\n        <a href="#cite_note-100">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Harvey">\n        Hurricane Harvey\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Hurricane Harvey">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">\n         Category 4\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017-08-25_2231Z.png">\n            <img alt="Harvey 2017-08-25 2231Z.png" data-file-height="2400" data-file-width="1800" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Harvey_2017-08-25_2231Z.png/150px-Harvey_2017-08-25_2231Z.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Harvey_2017-08-25_2231Z.png/225px-Harvey_2017-08-25_2231Z.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/04/Harvey_2017-08-25_2231Z.png/300px-Harvey_2017-08-25_2231Z.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Harvey_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Harvey 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Harvey_2017_track.png/150px-Harvey_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Harvey_2017_track.png/225px-Harvey_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Harvey_2017_track.png/300px-Harvey_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 17\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 1\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         130\xc2\xa0mph (215\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         938\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Harvey" title="Hurricane Harvey">\n        Hurricane Harvey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The NHC began monitoring an area of low pressure southwest of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Verde" title="Cape Verde">\n        Cape Verde\n       </a>\n       on August 13, which was expected to merge with a tropical wave that just emerged off the coast of Africa, within a few days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Instead the two systems remained separate,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-103">\n        <a href="#cite_note-103">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with the first low pressure area coalescing into a potential tropical cyclone by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa017.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A reconnaissance aircraft investigating the system was able to locate a well-defined circulation, and the disturbance was upgraded to Tropical Storm Harvey accordingly six hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On a westward course into the Caribbean Sea, the storm was plagued by relentless wind shear, and it degenerated to an open tropical wave south of Hispaniola, by 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa020.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">\n        <a href="#cite_note-106">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvey\'s remnants continued into the Bay of Campeche, where more conducive environmental conditions led to the re-designation of a tropical depression, around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa023, and subsequent intensification into a tropical storm by 04:00\xc2\xa0UTC on the next morning.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The tropical cyclone began a period of rapid intensification shortly thereafter, attaining hurricane intensity by 17:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa024,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_109-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-auto-109">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Category\xc2\xa03 strength around 19:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa025,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">\n        <a href="#cite_note-110">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and Category\xc2\xa04 intensity by 23:00\xc2\xa0UTC on that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-auto_109-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-auto-109">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Harvey crossed the shore between\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Aransas,_Texas" title="Port Aransas, Texas">\n        Port Aransas\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_O%27Connor,_Texas" title="Port O\'Connor, Texas">\n        Port O\'Connor, Texas\n       </a>\n       around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa026, possessing maximum winds of 130\xc2\xa0mph (215\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n        <a href="#cite_note-111">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm gradually spun down, becoming a tropical storm around 18:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa026, as it meandered across southeastern Texas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">\n        <a href="#cite_note-112">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A light steering pattern caused the storm to emerge into the Gulf of Mexico on August\xc2\xa028,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but a turn toward the north-northeast brought it ashore west of Cameron, Louisiana, as a weak tropical storm around 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n        <a href="#cite_note-114">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system weakened to a tropical depression over central Louisiana late that day before losing tropical characteristics over central Tennessee early on September\xc2\xa01.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Rockport,\n       <a href="/wiki/Fulton,_Texas" title="Fulton, Texas">\n        Fulton\n       </a>\n       , and the surrounding cities bore the brunt of Harvey\'s eyewall as it moved ashore in Texas. Numerous structures were heavily damaged or destroyed, boats were tossed or capsized, power poles were leant or snapped, and trees were downed. As debris covered roadways and cellphone service was compromised, communication to the hardest-hit locales was severed. One person was killed in Rockport after a fire began in his home, and approximately a dozen people were injured.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twc_117-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twc-117">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Farther northeast, dire predictions of potentially catastrophic flooding came to fruition in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Houston,_Texas" title="Houston, Texas">\n        Houston\n       </a>\n       and nearby locales, where floodwaters submerged interstates, forced residents to their attics and roofs, and overwhelmed emergency lines. The National Weather Service\n       <a href="/wiki/Twitter" title="Twitter">\n        tweeted\n       </a>\n       , "This event is unprecedented &amp; all impacts are unknown &amp; beyond anything experienced..." At least 30 people were killed in the Houston area due to flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TNYT_118-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TNYT-118">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition to the flooding, Harvey spawned several tornadoes around Houston.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">\n        <a href="#cite_note-119">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Estimates place the damage caused by Harvey at $198\xc2\xa0billion.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198billion_120-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-198billion-120">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvey killed 90 people, including 1 in\n       <a href="/wiki/Guyana" title="Guyana">\n        Guyana\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cdema_121-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-cdema-121">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and 89 in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122">\n        <a href="#cite_note-122">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WashPost_death_toll_123-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WashPost_death_toll-123">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-124">\n        <a href="#cite_note-124">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-125">\n        <a href="#cite_note-125">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm produced 64.58 in (1,640\xc2\xa0mm) of rainfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">\n        Texas\n       </a>\n       , the highest-ever rainfall total for any tropical cyclone in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-126">\n        <a href="#cite_note-126">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Harvey was the first major hurricane to strike the United States since Hurricane Wilma in 2005, ending the record-length 4,323-day span in which no tropical cyclones made landfall as major hurricanes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">\n        <a href="#cite_note-127">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It is the most intense tropical cyclone to move ashore the US mainland since Hurricane Charley in 2004, and the first Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane to make landfall in Texas since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Carla" title="Hurricane Carla">\n        Hurricane Carla\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/1961_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1961 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        1961\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">\n        <a href="#cite_note-128">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Irma">\n        Hurricane Irma\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Hurricane Irma">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff6060">\n         Category 5\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irma_2017-09-06_1745Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Irma 2017-09-06 1745Z.jpg" data-file-height="9600" data-file-width="7200" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Irma_2017-09-06_1745Z.jpg/150px-Irma_2017-09-06_1745Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Irma_2017-09-06_1745Z.jpg/225px-Irma_2017-09-06_1745Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4e/Irma_2017-09-06_1745Z.jpg/300px-Irma_2017-09-06_1745Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Irma_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Irma 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1669" data-file-width="2700" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Irma_2017_track.png/150px-Irma_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Irma_2017_track.png/225px-Irma_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0d/Irma_2017_track.png/300px-Irma_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         August 30\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 12\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         185\xc2\xa0mph (295\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         914\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irma" title="Hurricane Irma">\n        Hurricane Irma\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A westward-moving tropical wave, first monitored over western Africa on August\xc2\xa026,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">\n        <a href="#cite_note-129">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       organized into Tropical Storm Irma around 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on August\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">\n        <a href="#cite_note-130">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Amid an environment of low wind shear and warm ocean temperatures, the newly formed cyclone moved generally westward while intensifying. A reconnaissance aircraft investigating the system east of the Caribbean on September\xc2\xa05 found the cyclone at Category\xc2\xa05 intensity.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">\n        <a href="#cite_note-131">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       With a clear eye surrounded by a ring of extremely deep convection, Irma attained its peak intensity with winds of 185\xc2\xa0mph (295\xc2\xa0km/h) later that day,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">\n        <a href="#cite_note-132">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and maintained this intensity as it moved through the northern Leeward Islands.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-133">\n        <a href="#cite_note-133">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Some weakening occurred south of the Bahamas,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134">\n        <a href="#cite_note-134">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but the cyclone regained Category\xc2\xa05 intensity before making landfall on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Sabana-Camag%C3%BCey_Archipelago" title="Sabana-Camag\xc3\xbcey Archipelago">\n        Sabana-Camag\xc3\xbcey Archipelago\n       </a>\n       of Cuba around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa09.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-135">\n        <a href="#cite_note-135">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Land interaction disrupted the storm temporarily,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but once again it strengthened to acquire winds of 130\xc2\xa0mph (215\xc2\xa0km/h), before making landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cudjoe_Key,_Florida" title="Cudjoe Key, Florida">\n        Cudjoe Key\n       </a>\n       of the Florida Keys early on September\xc2\xa010.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-137">\n        <a href="#cite_note-137">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A few hours later, it struck\n       <a href="/wiki/Marco_Island,_Florida" title="Marco Island, Florida">\n        Marco Island, Florida\n       </a>\n       , with winds of 115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">\n        <a href="#cite_note-138">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Irma continued north and west, steadily weakening over the Southeastern United States before losing tropical characteristics in Georgia, early on September\xc2\xa012.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">\n        <a href="#cite_note-139">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       With peak winds of 185\xc2\xa0mph (295\xc2\xa0km/h), Irma is the strongest Atlantic storm outside of the Gulf of Mexico or Caribbean Sea on record, and is the 11th most intense hurricane on record in the Atlantic basin. Maintaining peak intensity for 37 consecutive hours, Irma is the only tropical cyclone on record worldwide to have had winds that intense for so long. As the storm moved through the northern Leeward Islands, it became the only Category\xc2\xa05 to make a direct impact there; its landfall intensity ties it with the 1935 Labor Day hurricane as the strongest landfalling cyclone on record in the Atlantic. Two Category\xc2\xa04 hurricanes, Harvey and Irma, struck the continental United States in the span of two weeks; this marks the first time the country has suffered two landfalls of such intensity during the same hurricane season, in recorded history. Lastly, Irma accrued the third-highest Accumulated Cyclone Energy index on record.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-140">\n        <a href="#cite_note-140">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the aftermath of Irma, development on the islands of\n       <a href="/wiki/Barbuda" title="Barbuda">\n        Barbuda\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Collectivity_of_Saint_Martin" title="Collectivity of Saint Martin">\n        Saint Martin\n       </a>\n       was described as being "95% destroyed" by respective political leaders, with 1,400 people feared homeless in Barbuda.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-141">\n        <a href="#cite_note-141">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       So far, Irma has resulted in at least 134 deaths, including 44 across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean" title="Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </a>\n       , and 90 in the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">\n        United States\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Reuters_death_toll_142-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Reuters_death_toll-142">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nuclear_landscape_143-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nuclear_landscape-143">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-World_AFP_death_toll_144-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-World_AFP_death_toll-144">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Jose">\n        Hurricane Jose\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Hurricane Jose">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff8f20">\n         Category 4\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jose_2017-09-08_1425Z_(cropped).jpg">\n            <img alt="Jose 2017-09-08 1425Z (cropped).jpg" data-file-height="454" data-file-width="319" height="213" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Jose_2017-09-08_1425Z_%28cropped%29.jpg/150px-Jose_2017-09-08_1425Z_%28cropped%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Jose_2017-09-08_1425Z_%28cropped%29.jpg/225px-Jose_2017-09-08_1425Z_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d9/Jose_2017-09-08_1425Z_%28cropped%29.jpg/300px-Jose_2017-09-08_1425Z_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Jose_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Jose 2017 track.png" data-file-height="2513" data-file-width="3000" height="126" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Jose_2017_track.png/150px-Jose_2017_track.png" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/33/Jose_2017_track.png/300px-Jose_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 5\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 22\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         155\xc2\xa0mph (250\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         938\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Jose_(2017)" title="Hurricane Jose (2017)">\n        Hurricane Jose (2017)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A westward-moving tropical wave exited the west coast of Africa on August\xc2\xa031,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-145">\n        <a href="#cite_note-145">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       organizing into Tropical Storm Jose over the open eastern Atlantic by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa05.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146">\n        <a href="#cite_note-146">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The quickly-strengthening cyclone attained hurricane intensity late on September\xc2\xa06,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">\n        <a href="#cite_note-147">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       reached major hurricane strength late on September\xc2\xa07,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">\n        <a href="#cite_note-148">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and ultimately peaked as a high-end Category\xc2\xa04 hurricane with winds of 155\xc2\xa0mph (250\xc2\xa0km/h) early on September\xc2\xa09.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">\n        <a href="#cite_note-149">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Moderate wind shear weakened the cyclone as it conducted a slow clockwise loop between Bermuda and the Caribbean Sea and eventually moved north ahead of an approaching trough.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">\n        <a href="#cite_note-150">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Steering currents collapsed by early on September\xc2\xa021, causing the system to stall offshore the Northeastern United States as a weakening tropical storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">\n        <a href="#cite_note-151">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       With a rain shield in the northern and northwestern semicircles accompanied by a lack of deep convection over the center, the NHC declared Jose a post-tropical cyclone around 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa022, ending advisories once the storm\'s tropical storm-force winds moved off the New England coast at 21:00 UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">\n        <a href="#cite_note-153">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The government of\n       <a href="/wiki/Antigua_and_Barbuda" title="Antigua and Barbuda">\n        Antigua and Barbuda\n       </a>\n       began efforts on September 8 to evacuate the entire island of Barbuda prior to Jose\'s anticipated arrival, as most structures on the island had been heavily damaged or destroyed by Hurricane Irma.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-154">\n        <a href="#cite_note-154">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Katia">\n        Hurricane Katia\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: Hurricane Katia">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffe775">\n         Category 2\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Katia_2017-09-08_1930Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Katia 2017-09-08 1930Z.jpg" data-file-height="5872" data-file-width="4536" height="194" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Katia_2017-09-08_1930Z.jpg/150px-Katia_2017-09-08_1930Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Katia_2017-09-08_1930Z.jpg/225px-Katia_2017-09-08_1930Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/38/Katia_2017-09-08_1930Z.jpg/300px-Katia_2017-09-08_1930Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Katia_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Katia 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Katia_2017_track.png/150px-Katia_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Katia_2017_track.png/225px-Katia_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/da/Katia_2017_track.png/300px-Katia_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 5\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 9\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         105\xc2\xa0mph (165\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         972\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katia_(2017)" title="Hurricane Katia (2017)">\n        Hurricane Katia (2017)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A trough was present over the southwestern Gulf of Mexico on September\xc2\xa03, producing a widespread area of thunderstorms.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-155">\n        <a href="#cite_note-155">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two days later, a distinct low pressure area formed about 50\xc2\xa0mi (80\xc2\xa0km) east of\n       <a href="/wiki/Tampico" title="Tampico">\n        Tampico\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Tamaulipas" title="Tamaulipas">\n        Tamaulipas\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-156">\n        <a href="#cite_note-156">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC that day, the NHC designated the system as Tropical Depression Thirteen after an organized area of convection formed over the center. Located in an area of weak steering currents, the depression drifted slowly eastward. With gradually decreasing wind shear and warm water temperatures, the system intensified into Tropical Storm Katia on September\xc2\xa06, as the convection became better organized.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">\n        <a href="#cite_note-157">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-158">\n        <a href="#cite_note-158">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later that day, an aircraft reconnaissance flight into the storm found a partial\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye wall\n       </a>\n       and surface winds of 76\xc2\xa0mph (122\xc2\xa0km/h); on that basis, the NHC upgraded Katia to hurricane status.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-159">\n        <a href="#cite_note-159">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The convection organized into a\n       <a href="/wiki/Central_dense_overcast" title="Central dense overcast">\n        central dense overcast\n       </a>\n       as the system stalled.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-160">\n        <a href="#cite_note-160">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Late in the evening of September 8, Katia made landfall north of\n       <a href="/wiki/Tecolutla" title="Tecolutla">\n        Tecolutla\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico">\n        Mexico\n       </a>\n       as a weak Category\xc2\xa01 storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-161">\n        <a href="#cite_note-161">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system rapidly dissipated over land on September 9. Katia\'s remnants traveled across Central America and later emerged over the Pacific Ocean, where redevelopment ensued. Tropical Depression Fifteen-E formed, which later strengthened into\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane_Otis_(2017)" title="Hurricane Otis (2017)">\n        Hurricane Otis\n       </a>\n       about a week later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-162">\n        <a href="#cite_note-162">\n         [159]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In preparation for Katia, over 4,000 residents were evacuated from the states of\n       <a href="/wiki/Veracruz" title="Veracruz">\n        Veracruz\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Puebla" title="Puebla">\n        Puebla\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-163">\n        <a href="#cite_note-163">\n         [160]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Tourists left coastal towns, emergency shelters were opened, and storm drains were cleared before the onset of heavy rainfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-164">\n        <a href="#cite_note-164">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two fatalities were reported in\n       <a href="/wiki/Xalapa" title="Xalapa">\n        Xalapa\n       </a>\n       from mudslides, while a third man was swept away by floodwaters in\n       <a href="/wiki/Jalcomulco" title="Jalcomulco">\n        Jalcomulco\n       </a>\n       . States of emergency were declared for 40 out of a total 53 municipalities that reported minor damage from mudslides and flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">\n        <a href="#cite_note-165">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       About 77,000 residents were left without power at the height of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-166">\n        <a href="#cite_note-166">\n         [163]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Lee">\n        Hurricane Lee\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Hurricane Lee">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffc140">\n         Category 3\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lee_2017-09-27_1450Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Lee 2017-09-27 1450Z.jpg" data-file-height="6000" data-file-width="4500" height="200" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Lee_2017-09-27_1450Z.jpg/150px-Lee_2017-09-27_1450Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Lee_2017-09-27_1450Z.jpg/225px-Lee_2017-09-27_1450Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/Lee_2017-09-27_1450Z.jpg/300px-Lee_2017-09-27_1450Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Lee_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Lee 2017 track.png" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="3000" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Lee_2017_track.png/150px-Lee_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Lee_2017_track.png/225px-Lee_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f9/Lee_2017_track.png/300px-Lee_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 15\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 30\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         962\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       A tropical wave moved off the coast of Africa on September 13. Contrary to predictions of only gradual organization over the following days,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-167">\n        <a href="#cite_note-167">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the system rapidly organized, becoming Tropical Depression Fourteen at 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September 15.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-168">\n        <a href="#cite_note-168">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The NHC upgraded the system to Tropical Storm Lee at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on the next day, based on an increase in deep convection and an\n       <a href="/wiki/Scatterometer" title="Scatterometer">\n        advanced scatterometer\n       </a>\n       (ASCAT) pass which indicated that it was producing minimal tropical-storm-force winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-169">\n        <a href="#cite_note-169">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After encountering wind shear, Lee gradually weakened into a tropical depression early on September\xc2\xa017 before degenerating into a remnant low two days later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170">\n        <a href="#cite_note-170">\n         [167]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171">\n        <a href="#cite_note-171">\n         [168]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The NHC monitored the remnants of Lee intermittently for several days, but regeneration was not considered likely.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">\n        <a href="#cite_note-172">\n         [169]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-173">\n        <a href="#cite_note-173">\n         [170]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, the mid-level remnants of the cyclone became intertwined with an upper-level trough; a deep burst of convection led to a new surface circulation, and by 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa022, the system reorganized into Tropical Depression Lee.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-174">\n        <a href="#cite_note-174">\n         [171]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It intensified into a tropical storm six hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175">\n        <a href="#cite_note-175">\n         [172]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       A compact cyclone, Lee organized as small curved bands wrapped into a small cluster of central convection.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176">\n        <a href="#cite_note-176">\n         [173]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A microwave pass around 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa023 indicated the formation of a ring of shallow to moderate convection around the center, often a harbinger of rapid intensification.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">\n        <a href="#cite_note-177">\n         [174]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Indeed, by 06:30\xc2\xa0UTC the next morning, the presence of an eye on satellite imagery prompted the NHC to abruptly upgrade Lee to a hurricane as it moved erratically.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">\n        <a href="#cite_note-178">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After attaining winds of 90\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h), the storm weakened slightly due to moderate southeasterly wind shear.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-179">\n        <a href="#cite_note-179">\n         [176]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa026, however, the storm attained Category\xc2\xa02 strength.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-180">\n        <a href="#cite_note-180">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An eyewall replacement cycle that night led to the emergence of a larger eye surrounded by cold cloud tops, and by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa027, Lee attained its peak as a Category\xc2\xa03 hurricane with winds of 115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-181">\n        <a href="#cite_note-181">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system recurved northeast after peak intensity and quickly succumbed to strong northerly wind shear and progressively cooler ocean waters;\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-182">\n        <a href="#cite_note-182">\n         [179]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       it weakened below major hurricane strength by 03:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa028,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">\n        <a href="#cite_note-183">\n         [180]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       fell below hurricane strength by 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa029,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-184">\n        <a href="#cite_note-184">\n         [181]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and degenerated to a post-tropical cyclone by 09:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa030, after lacking deep convection for over 12 hours.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-185">\n        <a href="#cite_note-185">\n         [182]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 1, Lee\'s remnant was absorbed by another extratropical cyclone to the north.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-October_1_weather_map_186-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-October_1_weather_map-186">\n         [183]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Maria">\n        Hurricane Maria\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Hurricane Maria">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ff6060">\n         Category 5\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Maria_2017-09-19_2015Z.png">\n            <img alt="Maria 2017-09-19 2015Z.png" data-file-height="1600" data-file-width="1600" height="150" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Maria_2017-09-19_2015Z.png/150px-Maria_2017-09-19_2015Z.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Maria_2017-09-19_2015Z.png/225px-Maria_2017-09-19_2015Z.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Maria_2017-09-19_2015Z.png/300px-Maria_2017-09-19_2015Z.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Maria_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Maria 2017 track.png" data-file-height="2290" data-file-width="3000" height="115" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Maria_2017_track.png/150px-Maria_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Maria_2017_track.png/225px-Maria_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Maria_2017_track.png/300px-Maria_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         September 16\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 September 30\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         175\xc2\xa0mph (280\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         908\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">\n        Hurricane Maria\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On September\xc2\xa013, the NHC began monitoring a tropical wave southwest of Cape Verde.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187">\n        <a href="#cite_note-187">\n         [184]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disturbance moved west, organizing into a potential tropical cyclone at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa016 and Tropical Storm Maria six hours later.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188">\n        <a href="#cite_note-188">\n         [185]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189">\n        <a href="#cite_note-189">\n         [186]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On a west-northwest course, Maria intensified at an exceptional rate; over a 24-hour period ending at 23:45\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa018, Maria doubled its winds from 80\xc2\xa0mph (130\xc2\xa0km/h) to 160\xc2\xa0mph (260\xc2\xa0km/h), thus reaching Category\xc2\xa05 strength.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190">\n        <a href="#cite_note-190">\n         [187]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After striking Dominica at that intensity a little over an hour later,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191">\n        <a href="#cite_note-191">\n         [188]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the storm weakened slightly as it entered the eastern Caribbean Sea; amid favorable conditions, however, Maria regained Category\xc2\xa05 intensity and eventually reached peak winds of 175\xc2\xa0mph (280\xc2\xa0km/h) late on September\xc2\xa019.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192">\n        <a href="#cite_note-192">\n         [189]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Around 08:00\xc2\xa0UTC on September\xc2\xa020, the eyewall of Maria struck\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vieques" title="Vieques">\n        Vieques\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193">\n        <a href="#cite_note-193">\n         [190]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and a little over two hours later, the core of the storm made landfall near\n       <a href="/wiki/Yabucoa,_Puerto_Rico" title="Yabucoa, Puerto Rico">\n        Yabucoa, Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       , with winds of 155\xc2\xa0mph (250\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194">\n        <a href="#cite_note-194">\n         [191]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Land interaction caused a significant degration in Maria\'s structure, and it weakened to a Category\xc2\xa02 hurricane while moving offshore.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-195">\n        <a href="#cite_note-195">\n         [192]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Growing in size and curving north, Maria regained Category\xc2\xa03 strength and maintained this intensity for several days before entering a less conducive environment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196">\n        <a href="#cite_note-196">\n         [193]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After fluctuating between tropical storm and minimal hurricane strength off the coastline of North Carolina,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197">\n        <a href="#cite_note-197">\n         [194]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       the system turned sharply east away from the United States, and ultimately evolved into an extratropical cyclone over the far northern Atlantic, on September\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198">\n        <a href="#cite_note-198">\n         [195]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199">\n        <a href="#cite_note-199">\n         [196]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Dominica sustained catastrophic damage from Maria, with nearly every structure on the island damaged or destroyed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200">\n        <a href="#cite_note-200">\n         [197]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Surrounding islands were also dealt a devastating blow, with reports of flooding, downed trees, and damaged buildings. Puerto Rico also suffered catastrophic damage. The island\'s electric grid was devastated, leaving all 3.4 million residents without power. Many structures were leveled, while floodwaters trapped thousands of citizens. The United States National Guard, Coast Guard, Army Corps of Engineers, and other like units worked to administer aid and assist in search and rescue operations. However, the U.S. federal government response was criticized for its delay in waiving the\n       <a href="/wiki/Merchant_Marine_Act_of_1920" title="Merchant Marine Act of 1920">\n        Jones Act\n       </a>\n       , a statute which prevented Puerto Rico from receiving aid on ships from non-U.S. flagged vessels. Along the coastline of the United States, tropical storm-force gusts cut power to hundreds of citizens; rip currents offshore led to three deaths and numerous water rescues. Estimates of damage from Maria range from $15.9 billion by Estudios T\xc3\xa9cnicos to $95 billion by\n       <a href="/wiki/Moody%27s_Analytics" title="Moody\'s Analytics">\n        Moody\'s Analytics\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MariaDamageEstimate_201-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MariaDamageEstimate-201">\n         [198]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most of the damage occurred in Puerto Rico; Ricardo Rossell\xc3\xb3, the governor of Puerto Rico, believes the storm caused $90 billion in damages.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90_billion_202-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90_billion-202">\n         [199]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The death toll currently stands at 97, with 28 killed in Dominica, 5 in the Dominican Republic, 2 in Guadeloupe, 3 in Haiti, 54 in Puerto Rico, 1 in the United States Virgin Islands, and 4 in the Contiguous United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43_in_Puerto_Rico_203-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43_in_Puerto_Rico-203">\n         [200]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The civilians in Puerto Rico reported that 583 people had died on the island since Hurricane Maria, and San Juan Mayor Yul\xc3\xadn Cruz said that the actual number of storm-related fatalities may be as high as 500, which indicates an unofficial death toll of 583.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10_times_higher_204-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10_times_higher-204">\n         [201]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Nate">\n        Hurricane Nate\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Hurricane Nate">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffffcc">\n         Category 1\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nate_2017-10-07_1848Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Nate 2017-10-07 1848Z.jpg" data-file-height="6272" data-file-width="4808" height="196" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Nate_2017-10-07_1848Z.jpg/150px-Nate_2017-10-07_1848Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Nate_2017-10-07_1848Z.jpg/225px-Nate_2017-10-07_1848Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Nate_2017-10-07_1848Z.jpg/300px-Nate_2017-10-07_1848Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nate_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Nate 2017 track.png" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="3000" height="150"
