     <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 4\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 9\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         90\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         981\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Nate_(2017)" title="Hurricane Nate (2017)">\n        Hurricane Nate (2017)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On October\xc2\xa03, a broad area of low pressure formed in the southwestern Caribbean Sea.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-205">\n        <a href="#cite_note-205">\n         [202]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The disturbance quickly organized, and on October 4, the NHC announced that the disturbance had strengthened into Tropical Depression Sixteen, and began issuing advisories on the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-206">\n        <a href="#cite_note-206">\n         [203]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system slowly became stronger and more organized, and, early on October 5, was deemed a tropical storm and named Nate.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-207">\n        <a href="#cite_note-207">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nate\'s first U.S landfall was in the mouth of the Mississippi River as a Category 1 hurricane, and Nate\'s second U.S landfall was at 12:30 a.m. CST near Biloxi, MS, both on October 8. After Nate tracked inland, it quickly weakened into a tropical depression, and a few hours later, evolved into an extratropical storm. Hurricane Nate also broke the record for the fastest moving hurricane ever recorded in the Gulf of Mexico.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fastest_storm_in_Gulf_208-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fastest_storm_in_Gulf-208">\n         [205]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Nate caused at least 40 deaths, including 16 in Nicaragua,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC_209-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC-209">\n         [206]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       11 in Costa Rica,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bohemia_1006_210-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Bohemia_1006-210">\n         [207]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       7 in Panama,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ElMundo_1006_211-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ElMundo_1006-211">\n         [208]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       3 in Honduras,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ElMundo_1006_211-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ElMundo_1006-211">\n         [208]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       1 in El Salvador,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ElMundo_1006_211-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ElMundo_1006-211">\n         [208]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and 2 in the United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-212">\n        <a href="#cite_note-212">\n         [209]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-213">\n        <a href="#cite_note-213">\n         [210]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hurricane_Ophelia">\n        Hurricane Ophelia\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Hurricane Ophelia">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #ffc140">\n         Category 3\xc2\xa0hurricane\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ophelia_2017-10-14_1454Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Ophelia 2017-10-14 1454Z.jpg" data-file-height="4808" data-file-width="3736" height="193" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Ophelia_2017-10-14_1454Z.jpg/150px-Ophelia_2017-10-14_1454Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Ophelia_2017-10-14_1454Z.jpg/225px-Ophelia_2017-10-14_1454Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e2/Ophelia_2017-10-14_1454Z.jpg/300px-Ophelia_2017-10-14_1454Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ophelia_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Ophelia 2017 track.png" data-file-height="2162" data-file-width="3000" height="108" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Ophelia_2017_track.png/150px-Ophelia_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Ophelia_2017_track.png/225px-Ophelia_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/Ophelia_2017_track.png/300px-Ophelia_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 9\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 16\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         960\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ophelia_(2017)" title="Hurricane Ophelia (2017)">\n        Hurricane Ophelia (2017)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On October\xc2\xa06, a circulation developed at the end of a cold front in the northeast Atlantic, with a low pressure area developing within the circulation on the same day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-214">\n        <a href="#cite_note-214">\n         [211]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While the low drifted slowly to the northeast, it began to lose its frontal system and acquire subtropical characteristics by October 7.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-215">\n        <a href="#cite_note-215">\n         [212]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The next day, the storm encountered stronger wind shear, removing some of its convection, and slightly weakening the system; however, the storm eventually grew better organized and developed more convection around its low pressure center later in the day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-216">\n        <a href="#cite_note-216">\n         [213]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on October 9, the system fully transitioned into a tropical cyclone, prompting the NHC to begin issuing advisories on Tropical Depression Seventeen.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-217">\n        <a href="#cite_note-217">\n         [214]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-218">\n        <a href="#cite_note-218">\n         [215]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The tropical depression continued to strengthen, becoming Tropical Storm Ophelia later that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219">\n        <a href="#cite_note-219">\n         [216]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ophelia continued to strengthen due to low wind shear and on October 11, the National Hurricane Center upgraded it to a hurricane, making it the tenth consecutive storm this season to reach hurricane strength.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-220">\n        <a href="#cite_note-220">\n         [217]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Ophelia became a Category 2 hurricane on October 12 at 5:00\xc2\xa0p.m. AST (21:00 UTC).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-221">\n        <a href="#cite_note-221">\n         [218]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 14 at 11:00\xc2\xa0a.m. AST (15:00 UTC), Ophelia unexpectedly intensified to a Category 3 hurricane, making Ophelia the sixth major hurricane of the season and the easternmost storm of such strength in the Atlantic basin on record.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RecordEast_222-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-RecordEast-222">\n         [219]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 15, Ophelia began to weaken, while accelerating northeastward towards\n       <a href="/wiki/Ireland" title="Ireland">\n        Ireland\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Great_Britain" title="Great Britain">\n        Great Britain\n       </a>\n       , with the storm\'s wind field also expanding. Early on October 16, Ophelia transitioned into a hurricane-strength extratropical cyclone, as it began impacting Ireland and Britain.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/County_Waterford" title="County Waterford">\n        County Waterford\n       </a>\n       , a woman was killed when a tree fell on her car, caused by the winds from Ophelia\'s remnants.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-223">\n        <a href="#cite_note-223">\n         [220]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/County_Tipperary" title="County Tipperary">\n        County Tipperary\n       </a>\n       , a man was killed while clearing a fallen tree with a chainsaw.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-224">\n        <a href="#cite_note-224">\n         [221]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Another person was killed in\n       <a href="/wiki/Dundalk" title="Dundalk">\n        Dundalk\n       </a>\n       when a tree fell on his car.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-225">\n        <a href="#cite_note-225">\n         [222]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Two other men died after suffering fatal injuries while carrying out repairs to damage caused by Ophelia and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Storm_Brian" title="Storm Brian">\n        Storm Brian\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-independent.ie_226-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-independent.ie-226">\n         [223]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hurricane Ophelia also fanned\n       <a href="/wiki/October_2017_Iberian_wildfires" title="October 2017 Iberian wildfires">\n        wildfires in Portugal and Spain\n       </a>\n       , killing 49 people.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-227">\n        <a href="#cite_note-227">\n         [224]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Philippe">\n        Tropical Storm Philippe\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Philippe">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;width: 24em;">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;font-weight: bold; background: #00faf4">\n         Tropical storm\xc2\xa0(SSHWS)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center">\n         <div style="vertical-align: middle">\n          <span class="nowrap">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Philippe_2017-10-28_1854Z.jpg">\n            <img alt="Philippe 2017-10-28 1854Z.jpg" data-file-height="2990" data-file-width="2216" height="202" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Philippe_2017-10-28_1854Z.jpg/150px-Philippe_2017-10-28_1854Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Philippe_2017-10-28_1854Z.jpg/225px-Philippe_2017-10-28_1854Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1d/Philippe_2017-10-28_1854Z.jpg/300px-Philippe_2017-10-28_1854Z.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n           <span class="nowrap">\n           </span>\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Philippe_2017_track.png">\n            <img alt="Philippe 2017 track.png" data-file-height="1854" data-file-width="3000" height="93" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Philippe_2017_track.png/150px-Philippe_2017_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Philippe_2017_track.png/225px-Philippe_2017_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/59/Philippe_2017_track.png/300px-Philippe_2017_track.png 2x" width="150"/>\n           </a>\n          </span>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Duration\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         October 28\xc2\xa0\xe2\x80\x93 October 29\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         Peak intensity\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         60\xc2\xa0mph (95\xc2\xa0km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min)\n         </small>\n         997\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On October\xc2\xa022, the NHC forecasted that a broad area of low pressure would form in the southwestern\n       <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Sea" title="Caribbean Sea">\n        Caribbean Sea\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228">\n        <a href="#cite_note-228">\n         [225]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 23, as predicted, a broad low formed off of the northwestern coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Nicaragua" title="Nicaragua">\n        Nicaragua\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-229">\n        <a href="#cite_note-229">\n         [226]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, the system remained disorganized for the next several days\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-230">\n        <a href="#cite_note-230">\n         [227]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       until the afternoon of October\xc2\xa027, when it quickly organized, prompting the NHC to upgrade the system into Potential Tropical Cyclone Eighteen. Slow development occurred over the next day, but the storm was ultimately deemed a tropical depression at 15:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October 28, after it developed a well-defined low-level circulation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-231">\n        <a href="#cite_note-231">\n         [228]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Continued strengthening occurred throughout the day as it moved over Cuba, becoming Tropical Storm Philippe near\n       <a href="/wiki/Havana" title="Havana">\n        Havana\n       </a>\n       about six hours later. Shortly thereafter, Philippe became poorly organized as it interacted with a non-tropical area of low pressure and a cold front, with the circulation becoming elongated, with three vortices existing within a broader low-level circulation. Philippe then made landfall over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Everglades" title="Everglades">\n        Everglades\n       </a>\n       in southwest\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">\n        Florida\n       </a>\n       with winds of 45 mph at around 9:00\xc2\xa0UTC on October 29. Effects were relatively minor in Florida although Philippe did spawn a few weak\n       <a href="/wiki/Tornado" title="Tornado">\n        tornadoes\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-232">\n        <a href="#cite_note-232">\n         [229]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       including one in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/West_Palm_Beach" title="West Palm Beach">\n        West Palm Beach\n       </a>\n       , and another in\n       <a href="/wiki/Miami" title="Miami">\n        Miami\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-233">\n        <a href="#cite_note-233">\n         [230]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After crossing the southern Florida Peninsula, Philippe began to intensify over the open Atlantic reaching a peak strength of 60 mph. However, by 21:00\xc2\xa0UTC, Philippe dissipated, as the circulation merged with a cold front that was part of a larger extratropical cyclone, which was bringing heavy rain and wind to the Northeastern United States and\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Canada" title="Eastern Canada">\n        Eastern Canada\n       </a>\n       . Philippe did not become a hurricane, thus ending a record-tying period with 10 consecutive hurricanes (with winds of at least 75 mph).\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The combination of Philippe and the extratropical system resulted in approximately 1.2\xc2\xa0million power outages in New England. The system produced storm-force sustained winds, reaching 57\xc2\xa0mph (92\xc2\xa0km/h) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Warwick,_Rhode_Island" title="Warwick, Rhode Island">\n        Warwick, Rhode Island\n       </a>\n       , and hurricane-force wind gusts, peaking at 93\xc2\xa0mph (150\xc2\xa0km/h) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Popponesset,_Massachusetts" title="Popponesset, Massachusetts">\n        Popponesset, Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-234">\n        <a href="#cite_note-234">\n         [231]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-235">\n        <a href="#cite_note-235">\n         [232]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Canada,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hydro-Qu%C3%A9bec" title="Hydro-Qu\xc3\xa9bec">\n        Hydro-Qu\xc3\xa9bec\n       </a>\n       reported 200,000 customers losing power because of damages due to winds of 70 to 90 kilometres per hour (43 to 56\xc2\xa0mph). It also rained heavily in\n       <a href="/wiki/Quebec" title="Quebec">\n        Quebec\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Ontario" title="Eastern Ontario">\n        Eastern Ontario\n       </a>\n       , with up to 98 millimetres (3.9\xc2\xa0in) in the Canadian capital region of\n       <a href="/wiki/Ottawa" title="Ottawa">\n        Ottawa\n       </a>\n       forcing Prime Minister\n       <a href="/wiki/Justin_Trudeau" title="Justin Trudeau">\n        Justin Trudeau\n       </a>\n       to use an all-terrain vehicle to leave from his second home on Mousseau Lake in\n       <a href="/wiki/Gatineau_Park" title="Gatineau Park">\n        Gatineau Park\n       </a>\n       to go to Parliament.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LP_236-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-LP-236">\n         [233]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tropical_Storm_Rina">\n        Tropical Storm Rina\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Tropical Storm Rina">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="infobox" style="width:22em;border-collapse:collapse; -48.3\n              </span>\n             </span>\n             <span style="display:none">\n              \xef\xbb\xbf (\n              <span class="fn org">\n               Tropical Storm Rina\n              </span>\n              )\n             </span>\n            </span>\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </span>\n         \xc2\xb1 30\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nautical_miles" title="Nautical miles">\n          nm\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         About 375 mi (600 km)\n         <a href="/wiki/Points_of_the_compass" title="Points of the compass">\n          SE\n         </a>\n         of\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_Race,_Newfoundland" title="Cape Race, Newfoundland">\n          Cape Race, Newfoundland\n         </a>\n         , About 1160 mi (1870 km)\n         <a href="/wiki/Points_of_the_compass" title="Points of the compass">\n          WNW\n         </a>\n         of the\n         <a href="/wiki/Azores" title="Azores">\n          Azores\n         </a>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">\n         Sustained winds:\n        </th>\n        <td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">\n         45 kt (50 mph; 85 km/h)\n         <small>\n          (1-min mean)\n         </small>\n         <br/>\n         gusting to 55 kt (65 mph; 100 km/h)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">\n         Pressure:\n        </th>\n        <td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">\n         995\n         <a href="/wiki/Bar_(unit)" title="Bar (unit)">\n          mbar\n         </a>\n         (\n         <a href="/wiki/Pascal_(unit)" title="Pascal (unit)">\n          hPa\n         </a>\n         ; 29.39\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Inches_of_Mercury" title="Inches of Mercury">\n          inHg\n         </a>\n         )\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row" style="padding-left:0.3em; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">\n         Movement:\n        </th>\n        <td style="width:80%; border-top: #aaa 1px solid;">\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Points_on_the_compass" title="Points on the compass">\n          NNE\n         </a>\n         at 20 kt (23 mph; 37 km/h)\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="2" style="text-align:center;border-top:#aaa 1px solid; background: #00faf4;">\n         <dl>\n          <dt>\n           <b>\n            See more\n            <a href="#Current_storm_information">\n             detailed information\n            </a>\n            .\n           </b>\n          </dt>\n         </dl>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       In early November, the National Hurricane Center began to monitor a non-tropical area of low pressure in the central Atlantic, which had formed at the end of a decaying cold front, for potential tropical development. Gradually, the system became better organized and was able to maintain an area of deep convection to the east of the center. On the morning of November 6, the NHC declared that Tropical Depression Nineteen had formed in the Central Atlantic.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-237">\n        <a href="#cite_note-237">\n         [234]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the day progressed, wind shear from the west began to impact the tropical cyclone, displacing shower and thunderstorm activity to the east. Despite this, the system continued to strengthen, and by 03:00 UTC on November 7, the tropical depression was upgraded to a tropical storm, gaining the name Rina.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-238">\n        <a href="#cite_note-238">\n         [235]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Current_storm_information">\n        Current storm information\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Current storm information">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       As of 11:00\xc2\xa0p.m.\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atlantic_Standard_Time" title="Atlantic Standard Time">\n        AST\n       </a>\n       November 8 (03:00\n       <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       November\xc2\xa09), Tropical Storm Rina is located within 30\xc2\xa0nautical miles of\n       <span class="plainlinks nourlexpansion">\n        <a class="external text" href="//tools.wmflabs.org/geohack/geohack.php?pagename=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;params=42.5_N_-48.3_E_dim:280km&amp;title=Rina">\n         <span class="geo-nondefault">\n          <span class="geo-dms" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">\n           <span class="latitude">\n            42\xc2\xb030\xe2\x80\xb2N\n           </span>\n           <span class="longitude">\n            48\xc2\xb018\xe2\x80\xb2W\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </span>\n         <span class="geo-multi-punct">\n          \xef\xbb\xbf / \xef\xbb\xbf\n         </span>\n         <span class="geo-default">\n          <span class="vcard">\n           <span class="geo-dec" title="Maps, aerial photos, and other data for this location">\n            42.5\xc2\xb0N 48.3\xc2\xb0W\n           </span>\n           <span style="display:none">\n            \xef\xbb\xbf /\n            <span class="geo">\n             42.5; -48.3\n            </span>\n           </span>\n           <span style="display:none">\n            \xef\xbb\xbf (\n            <span class="fn org">\n             Rina\n            </span>\n            )\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </span>\n        </a>\n       </span>\n       , about 375\xc2\xa0miles (600\xc2\xa0km) southeast of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cape_Race,_Newfoundland" title="Cape Race, Newfoundland">\n        Cape Race, Newfoundland\n       </a>\n       and about 1160\xc2\xa0miles (1870\xc2\xa0km) southeast of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Azores" title="Azores">\n        Azores\n       </a>\n       . Maximum sustained winds are 45\xc2\xa0knots (50\xc2\xa0mph; 85\xc2\xa0km/h), with gusts to 55\xc2\xa0knots (65\xc2\xa0mph; 100\xc2\xa0km/h). The minimum barometric pressure is 995\xc2\xa0millibars (hPa; 29.38\xc2\xa0inHg). The system is moving north-northeast at 20\xc2\xa0knots (23\xc2\xa0mph; 37\xc2\xa0km/h). Tropical-storm-force winds extend outward up to 205 miles (335\xc2\xa0kilometres), mainly to the east of the center.\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       For latest official information, see:\n      </p>\n      <ul>\n       <li>\n        The NHC\'s\n        <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/text/refresh/MIATCPAT4+shtml/" rel="nofollow">\n         latest public advisory on Tropical Storm Rina\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The NHC\'s\n        <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/text/refresh/MIATCMAT4+shtml/" rel="nofollow">\n         latest forecast advisory on Tropical Storm Rina\n        </a>\n       </li>\n       <li>\n        The NHC\'s\n        <a class="external text" href="http://www.nhc.noaa.gov/text/refresh/MIATCDAT4+shtml/" rel="nofollow">\n         latest forecast discussion on Tropical Storm Rina\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Other_systems">\n        Other systems\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Other systems">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="7057" data-file-width="5025" height="239" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg/170px-10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg/255px-10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4a/10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg/340px-10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg 2x" width="170"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:10L_2017-08-28_1750Z.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Potential Tropical Cyclone Ten near the Carolinas on August 28\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A long-tracked tropical wave was designated as Potential Tropical Cyclone Ten on August 27, while it was located northeast of Florida. The NHC gave this disturbance a 90% chance of becoming a tropical cyclone within the next 48 hours.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-239">\n        <a href="#cite_note-239">\n         [236]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The system reached sustained wind speeds of 45 miles per hour and affected the East Coast. However, the system did not acquire any more tropical characteristics, and it began to undergo an extratropical transition. Consequently, the NHC issued its last advisory on the system at 21:00 UTC on August 29, declaring the system to be an extratropical low.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-240">\n        <a href="#cite_note-240">\n         [237]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Storm_names">\n        Storm names\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Storm names">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main articles:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        Tropical cyclone naming\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/History_of_tropical_cyclone_naming" title="History of tropical cyclone naming">\n        History of tropical cyclone naming\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_historic_tropical_cyclone_names" title="List of historic tropical cyclone names">\n        List of historic tropical cyclone names\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The following list of names will be used for named storms that form in the North Atlantic in 2017. Any retired names will be announced by the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        World Meteorological Organization\n       </a>\n       (WMO) in the spring of 2018. The names not retired from this list will not be used again until the 2023 season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-241">\n        <a href="#cite_note-241">\n         [238]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This is the same list used in the\n       <a href="/wiki/2011_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2011 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2011 season\n       </a>\n       , with the exception of the name Irma, which replaced\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irene" title="Hurricane Irene">\n        Irene\n       </a>\n       ; Irma was previously used in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Irma_(1978)" title="Tropical Storm Irma (1978)">\n        1978 season\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <table style="width:90%;">\n       <tr>\n </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div style="clear:both;">\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The usage of the name "Don" in July garnered some attention relating to\n       <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">\n        United States President\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">\n        Donald Trump\n       </a>\n       .\n       <a href="/wiki/Max_Mayfield" title="Max Mayfield">\n        Max Mayfield\n       </a>\n       , former director of the National Hurricane Center, clarified that the name had no relation to Trump and was chosen in 2006 as a replacement for\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dennis" title="Hurricane Dennis">\n        Dennis\n       </a>\n       . Regardless, some outlets such as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Associated_Press" title="Associated Press">\n        Associated Press\n       </a>\n       , "poked fun" at the name and Trump.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-242">\n        <a href="#cite_note-242">\n         [239]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-243">\n        <a href="#cite_note-243">\n         [240]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Season_effects">\n        Season effects\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Season effects">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       This is a table of all the storms that have formed in the 2017 Atlantic hurricane season. It includes their duration, names, affected areas, damages, and death totals. Deaths in parentheses are additional and indirect (an example of an indirect death would be a traffic accident), but were still related to that storm. Damage and deaths include totals while the storm was extratropical, a wave, or a low, and all the damage figures are in 2017\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USD" title="USD">\n        USD\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <table align="center" border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="background:transparent;text-align:center">\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="7" </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Footnotes">\n        Footnotes\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Footnotes">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">\n       <div class="mw-references-wrap">\n        <ol class="references">\n         <li id="cite_note-25">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-25">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           There is an undercount bias of zero to six tropical cyclones per year between 1851 and 1885 and zero to four per year between 1886 and 1910, due to the lack of modern observation techniques, see\n           <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_observation" title="Tropical cyclone observation">\n            Tropical cyclone observation\n           </a>\n           . This may have led to significantly lower ACE ratings for hurricane seasons prior to 1910.\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NOAA1_23-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-NOAA1-23">\n             [23]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NOAA2_24-0">\n            <a href="#cite_note-NOAA2-24">\n             [24]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </span>\n         </li>\n         <li id="cite_note-27">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-27">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           The totals represent the sum of the squares for every (sub)tropical storm\'s intensity of over 33\xc2\xa0knots (38\xc2\xa0mph, 61\xc2\xa0km/h), divided by 10,000. Calculations are provided at\n           <a href="/wiki/Talk:2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season/ACE_calcs" title="Talk:2017 Atlantic hurricane season/ACE calcs">\n            Talk:2017 Atlantic hurricane season/ACE calcs\n           </a>\n           .\n          </span>\n         </li>\n         <li id="cite_note-34">\n          <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n           <b>\n            <a href="#cite_ref-34">\n             ^\n            </a>\n           </b>\n          </span>\n          <span class="reference-text">\n           It should be noted that Arlene would likely not have been detected without the help of satellites, and there may well have been other similar storms this early in the year in the pre-satellite era (1966 and before).\n           <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-33">\n            <a href="#cite_note-33">\n             [31]\n            </a>\n           </sup>\n          </span>\n         </li>\n        </ol>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="References">\n        References\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=2017_Atlantic_hurricane_season&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: References">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="reflist columns references-column-width" style="-moz-column-width: 30em;
